<div  id="description" slot="content"><yt-formatted-string  id="description" split-lines=""><span  dir="auto">Hindustani Classical Music is the art music of northern regions of the Indian subcontinent. It may also be called North Indian classical music or Sastriya Sangit. Its origins date from the 12th century CE, when it diverged from Carnatic music, the classical tradition of southern regions of the Indian subcontinent.
